::centre
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa
::

# Vinayapiṭake

## Parivārapāḷi

#### 1. Bhikkhuvibhaṅgo

### Soḷasamahāvāro

#### 1. Katthapaññattivāro

#### 1. Pārājikakaṇḍaṃ

{para:1} 1\. Yaṃ {pb:T:0.0001}{pb:P:5.0001}{pb:M:0.0001}{pb:V:0.0001} tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena paṭhamaṃ pārājikaṃ kattha paññattaṃ, kaṃ ārabbha, kismiṃ vatthusmiṃ? Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññatti? Sabbatthapaññatti, padesapaññatti? Sādhāraṇapaññatti, asādhāraṇapaññatti? Ekatopaññatti, ubhatopaññatti? Pañcannaṃ pātimokkhuddesānaṃ katthogadhaṃ kattha pariyāpannaṃ? Katamena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchati? Catunnaṃ vipattīnaṃ katamā vipatti? Sattannaṃ āpattikkhandhānaṃ {pb:V:0.0002} katamo āpattikkhandho? Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti? Catunnaṃ adhikaraṇānaṃ katamaṃ adhikaraṇaṃ? Sattannaṃ samathānaṃ katihi samathehi sammati? Ko tattha vinayo, ko tattha abhivinayo? Kiṃ tattha pātimokkhaṃ, kiṃ tattha adhipātimokkhaṃ? Kā vipatti? Kā sampatti? Kā paṭipatti? Kati atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā paṭhamaṃ pārājikaṃ paññattaṃ? Ke sikkhanti? Ke sikkhitasikkhā? Kattha ṭhitaṃ? Ke dhārenti? Kassa vacanaṃ? Kenābhatanti?

{para:2} 2\. Yaṃ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena paṭhamaṃ {pb:T:0.0002} pārājikaṃ kattha paññattanti? Vesāliyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sudinnaṃ kalandaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sudinno kalandaputto purāṇadutiyikāya methunaṃ {pb:P:5.0002} dhammaṃ paṭisevi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññattīti? Ekā paññatti, dve anupaññattiyo. Anuppannapaññatti {pb:M:0.0002} tasmiṃ natthi. Sabbatthapaññatti, padesapaññattīti? Sabbatthapaññatti. Sādhāraṇapaññatti, asādhāraṇapaññattīti? Sādhāraṇapaññatti. Ekatopaññatti, ubhatopaññattīti? Ubhatopaññatti. Pañcannaṃ pātimokkhuddesānaṃ katthogadhaṃ kattha pariyāpannanti? Nidānogadhaṃ, nidānapariyāpannaṃ. Katamena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchatīti? Dutiyena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchati. Catunnaṃ vipattīnaṃ katamā vipattīti? Sīlavipatti. Sattannaṃ āpattikkhandhānaṃ katamo āpattikkhandhoti? Pārājikāpattikkhandho. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhātīti? Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato. Catunnaṃ adhikaraṇānaṃ katamaṃ adhikaraṇanti? Āpattādhikaraṇaṃ. Sattannaṃ samathānaṃ katihi samathehi sammatīti? Dvīhi samathehi sammati – sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca. Ko tattha vinayo, ko tattha abhivinayoti? Paññatti vinayo, vibhatti abhivinayo. Kiṃ tattha pātimokkhaṃ, kiṃ tattha adhipātimokkhanti? Paññatti pātimokkhaṃ, vibhatti adhipātimokkhaṃ. Kā vipattīti? Asaṃvaro vipatti. Kā {pb:T:0.0003} sampattīti? Saṃvaro sampatti. Kā paṭipattīti? Na evarūpaṃ karissāmīti yāvajīvaṃ āpāṇakoṭikaṃ samādāya sikkhati sikkhāpadesu. {note:a. ni. 10.31} Kati atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā paṭhamaṃ pārājikaṃ paññattanti? Dasa atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā paṭhamaṃ pārājikaṃ paññattaṃ – saṅghasuṭṭhutāya, saṅghaphāsutāya, dummaṅkūnaṃ puggalānaṃ niggahāya, pesalānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ phāsuvihārāya, diṭṭhadhammikānaṃ āsavānaṃ saṃvarāya, samparāyikānaṃ āsavānaṃ paṭighātāya, appasannānaṃ pasādāya, pasannānaṃ bhiyyobhāvāya, saddhammaṭṭhitiyā, vinayānuggahāya. Ke sikkhantīti? Sekkhā ca puthujjanakalyāṇakā ca sikkhanti. Ke sikkhitasikkhāti? Arahanto sikkhitasikkhā{pb:V:0.0003}. Kattha ṭhitanti? Sikkhākāmesu ṭhitaṃ. Ke dhārentīti? Yesaṃ vattati te dhārenti. Kassa vacananti? Bhagavato vacanaṃ arahato sammāsambuddhassa. Kenābhatanti? Paramparābhataṃ –

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Upāli dāsako ceva, soṇako siggavo tathā;
::

::gathalast
Moggaliputtena {note:moggalīputtena (syā.)} pañcamā, ete jambusirivhaye {note:jambusarivhaye (sārattha)}.
::

::gatha1
Tato {pb:P:5.0003} mahindo iṭṭiyo {note:iṭṭhiyo (sī.)}, uttiyo sambalo {note:uṭṭiyo sampalo (itipi)} tathā;
::

::gathalast
Bhaddanāmo ca paṇḍito.
::

::gatha1
Ete {pb:M:0.0003} nāgā mahāpaññā, jambudīpā idhāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Vinayaṃ te vācayiṃsu, piṭakaṃ tambapaṇṇiyā.
::

::gatha1
Nikāye {pb:T:0.0004} pañca vācesuṃ, satta ceva pakaraṇe;
::

::gathalast
Tato ariṭṭho medhāvī, tissadatto ca paṇḍito.
::

::gatha1
Visārado kāḷasumano, thero ca dīghanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Dīghasumano ca paṇḍito.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva {note:punareva (syā.)} kāḷasumano, nāgatthero ca buddharakkhito;
::

::gathalast
Tissatthero ca medhāvī, devatthero {note:revatthero (itipi)} ca paṇḍito.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva {pb:V:0.0004} sumano medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado;
::

::gathalast
Bahussuto cūḷanāgo, gajova duppadhaṃsiyo.
::

::gatha1
Dhammapālitanāmo ca, rohaṇe {note:rohaṇo (sī.)} sādhupūjito;
::

::gathalast
Tassa sisso mahāpañño khemanāmo tipeṭako.
::

::gatha1
Dīpe tārakarājāva paññāya atirocatha;
::

::gathalast
Upatisso ca medhāvī, phussadevo mahākathī.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva sumano medhāvī, pupphanāmo bahussuto;
::

::gathalast
Mahākathī mahāsivo, piṭake sabbattha kovido.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva upāli medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado;
::

::gathalast
Mahānāgo mahāpañño, saddhammavaṃsakovido.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva abhayo medhāvī, piṭake sabbattha kovido;
::

::gathalast
Tissatthero ca medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado.
::

::gatha1
Tassa sisso mahāpañño, pupphanāmo bahussuto;
::

::gathalast
Sāsanaṃ {pb:T:0.0005} anurakkhanto, jambudīpe patiṭṭhito.
::

::gatha1
Cūḷābhayo ca medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado;
::

::gathalast
Tissatthero ca medhāvī, saddhammavaṃsakovido.
::

::gatha1
Cūḷadevo {note:phussadevo (sī.)} ca medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado;
::

::gathalast
Sivatthero ca medhāvī, vinaye sabbattha kovido.
::

::gatha1
Ete {pb:M:0.0004} nāgā mahāpaññā, vinayaññū maggakovidā;
::

::gathalast
Vinayaṃ dīpe pakāsesuṃ, piṭakaṃ tambapaṇṇiyāti.
::

{para:4} 4\. Yaṃ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena dutiyaṃ pārājikaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Dhaniyaṃ kumbhakāraputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Dhaniyo kumbhakāraputto rañño dārūni adinnaṃ ādiyi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhātīti? Tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti{pb:P:5.0004}, na vācato; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:5} 5\. Tatiyaṃ pārājikaṃ kattha paññattanti? Vesāliyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule {pb:V:0.0005} bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū aññamaññaṃ jīvitā voropesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ {pb:T:0.0006} āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhātīti? Tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:6} 6\. Catutthaṃ pārājikaṃ kattha paññattanti? Vesāliyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Vaggumudātīriye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Vaggumudātīriyā bhikkhū gihīnaṃ aññamaññassa uttarimanussadhammassa vaṇṇaṃ bhāsiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhātīti? Tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Cattāro pārājikā niṭṭhitā.
::

::centre
Tassuddānaṃ –
::

::gatha1
Methunādinnādānañca{pb:M:0.0005}, manussaviggahuttari;
::

::gathalast
Pārājikāni cattāri, chejjavatthū asaṃsayāti.
::

#### 2. Saṅghādisesakaṇḍaṃ

{para:7} 7\. Yaṃ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena upakkamitvā asuciṃ mocentassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññatto? Kaṃ ārabbha? Kismiṃ vatthusmiṃ? Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti{pb:T:0.0007}, anuppannapaññatti? Sabbatthapaññatti, padesapaññatti? Sādhāraṇapaññatti, asādhāraṇapaññatti? Ekatopaññatti, ubhatopaññatti? Pañcannaṃ pātimokkhuddesānaṃ katthogadhaṃ kattha pariyāpannaṃ? Katamena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchati? Catunnaṃ vipattīnaṃ katamā vipatti? Sattannaṃ āpattikkhandhānaṃ katamo āpattikkhandho? Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti? Catunnaṃ adhikaraṇānaṃ katamaṃ adhikaraṇaṃ? Sattannaṃ samathānaṃ katihi samathehi sammati? Ko tattha vinayo, ko tattha abhivinayo? Kiṃ tattha pātimokkhaṃ, kiṃ tattha adhipātimokkhaṃ{pb:V:0.0006}? Kā vipatti, kā sampatti, kā paṭipatti? Kati atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā upakkamitvā asuciṃ mocentassa saṅghādiseso paññatto? Ke sikkhanti, ke sikkhitasikkhā? Kattha ṭhitaṃ? Ke dhārenti? Kassa vacanaṃ? Kenābhatanti?

{para:8} 8\. Yaṃ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena upakkamitvā asuciṃ mocentassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ seyyasakaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā seyyasako hatthena upakkamitvā asuciṃ mocesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññattīti? Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Anuppannapaññatti tasmiṃ natthi. Sabbattha paññatti, padesapaññattīti? Sabbatthapaññatti. Sādhāraṇapaññatti, asādhāraṇapaññattīti{pb:T:0.0008}? Asādhāraṇapaññatti. Ekatopaññatti, ubhatopaññattīti? Ekatopaññatti. Pañcannaṃ pātimokkhuddesānaṃ katthogadhaṃ kattha pariyāpannanti? Nidānogadhaṃ nidānapariyāpannaṃ. Katamena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchatīti? Tatiye {pb:M:0.0006} uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchati{pb:P:5.0005}. Catunnaṃ vipattīnaṃ katamā vipattīti? Sīlavipatti. Sattannaṃ āpattikkhandhānaṃ katamo āpattikkhandhoti? Saṅghādiseso āpattikkhandho. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhātīti? Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato. Catunnaṃ adhikaraṇānaṃ katamaṃ adhikaraṇanti? Āpattādhikaraṇaṃ. Sattannaṃ samathānaṃ katihi samathehi sammatīti? Dvīhi samathehi sammati – sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca. Ko tattha vinayo, ko tattha abhivinayoti? Paññatti vinayo, vibhatti abhivinayo. Kiṃ tattha pātimokkhaṃ, kiṃ tattha adhipātimokkhanti? Paññatti pātimokkhaṃ, vibhatti adhipātimokkhaṃ. Kā vipattīti? Asaṃvaro vipatti. Kā sampattīti? Saṃvaro sampatti. Kā paṭipattīti? Na evarūpaṃ karissāmīti yāvajīvaṃ āpāṇakoṭikaṃ samādāya sikkhati sikkhāpadesu. {note:a. ni. 10.31} Kati atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā upakkamitvā asuciṃ mocentassa saṅghādiseso paññattoti? Dasa atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā upakkamitvā asuciṃ mocentassa saṅghādiseso paññatto – saṅghasuṭṭhutāya, saṅghaphāsutāya, dummaṅkūnaṃ puggalānaṃ niggahāya, pesalānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ phāsuvihārāya, diṭṭhadhammikānaṃ āsavānaṃ saṃvarāya, samparāyikānaṃ āsavānaṃ {pb:T:0.0009} paṭighātāya, appasannānaṃ pasādāya, pasannānaṃ bhiyyobhāvāya, saddhammaṭṭhitiyā, vinayānuggahāya. Ke sikkhantīti? Sekkhā ca puthujjanakalyāṇakā ca sikkhanti. Ke sikkhitasikkhāti? Arahanto sikkhitasikkhā. Kattha ṭhitanti? Sikkhākāmesu ṭhitaṃ. Ke dhārentīti? Yesaṃ vattati{pb:V:0.0007}, te dhārenti. Kassa vacananti? Bhagavato vacanaṃ arahato sammāsambuddhassa. Kenābhatanti? Paramparābhataṃ –
