{para:9} 9\. Yaṃ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena mātugāmena saddhiṃ kāyasaṃsaggaṃ samāpajjantassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha{pb:M:0.0008}. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā udāyī mātugāmena {pb:T:0.0010} saddhiṃ kāyasaṃsaggaṃ samāpajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:10} 10\. Mātugāmaṃ duṭṭhullāhi vācāhi obhāsantassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā {pb:V:0.0009} udāyī mātugāmaṃ duṭṭhullāhi vācāhi obhāsi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:11} 11\. Mātugāmassa santike attakāmapāricariyāya vaṇṇaṃ bhāsantassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā {pb:T:0.0011} udāyī mātugāmassa santike attakāmapāricariyāya vaṇṇaṃ abhāsi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:12} 12\. Sañcarittaṃ samāpajjantassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā udāyī sañcarittaṃ samāpajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; siyā vācato samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato na cittato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato; siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato{pb:P:5.0006}; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:13} 13\. Saññācikā {pb:M:0.0009} kuṭiṃ kārāpentassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Āḷaviyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āḷavake bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āḷavakā bhikkhū saññācikāya kuṭiyo kārāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:14} 14\. Mahallakaṃ vihāraṃ kārāpentassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Kosambiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ channaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā channo vihāravatthuṃ sodhento aññataraṃ cetiyarukkhaṃ chedāpesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:15} 15\. Bhikkhuṃ {pb:V:0.0010} amūlakena pārājikena dhammena anuddhaṃsentassa saṅghādiseso {pb:T:0.0012} kattha paññattoti? Rājagahe paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Mettiyabhūmajake bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Mettiyabhūmajakā bhikkhū āyasmantaṃ dabbaṃ mallaputtaṃ amūlakena pārājikena dhammena anuddhaṃsesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:16} 16\. Bhikkhuṃ aññabhāgiyassa adhikaraṇassa kiñci desaṃ lesamattaṃ upādāya pārājikena dhammena anuddhaṃsentassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Rājagahe paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Mettiyabhūmajake bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Mettiyabhūmajakā bhikkhū āyasmantaṃ dabbaṃ mallaputtaṃ aññabhāgiyassa adhikaraṇassa kiñci desaṃ lesamattaṃ upādāya pārājikena dhammena anuddhaṃsesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:17} 17\. Saṅghabhedakassa bhikkhuno yāvatatiyaṃ samanubhāsanāya na paṭinissajjantassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Rājagahe paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Devadattaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Devadatto samaggassa saṅghassa bhedāya parakkami, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:18} 18\. Bhedānuvattakānaṃ {pb:M:0.0010} bhikkhūnaṃ yāvatatiyaṃ samanubhāsanāya na paṭinissajjantānaṃ saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Rājagahe paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū devadattassa saṅghabhedāya parakkamantassa {pb:T:0.0013} anuvattakā ahesuṃ vaggavādakā, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:19} 19\. Dubbacassa bhikkhuno yāvatatiyaṃ samanubhāsanā {pb:P:5.0007} na paṭinissajjantassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Kosambiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ channaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā channo bhikkhūhi sahadhammikaṃ vuccamāno attānaṃ avacanīyaṃ akāsi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:20} 20\. Kuladūsakassa {pb:V:0.0011} bhikkhuno yāvatatiyaṃ samanubhāsanāya na paṭinissajjantassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Assajipunabbasuke bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Assajipunabbasukā bhikkhū saṅghena pabbājanīyakammakatā bhikkhū chandagāmitā dosagāmitā mohagāmitā bhayagāmitā pāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Terasa saṅghādisesā niṭṭhitā.
::

::centre
Tassuddānaṃ –
::

::gatha1
Vissaṭṭhi {pb:T:0.0014} kāyasaṃsaggaṃ, duṭṭhullaṃ attakāmañca;
::

::gathalast
Sañcarittaṃ kuṭī ceva, vihāro ca amūlakaṃ.
::

::gatha1
Kiñcidesañca bhedo ca, tasseva {note:tatheva (ka.)} anuvattakā;
::

::gathalast
Dubbacaṃ kuladūsañca, saṅghādisesā terasāti.
::

#### 3. Aniyatakaṇḍaṃ

{para:21} 21\. Yaṃ {pb:M:0.0011} tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena paṭhamo aniṃyato kattha paññatto? Kaṃ ārabbha? Kismiṃ vatthusmiṃ? Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññatti, sabbatthapaññatti padesapaññatti, sādhāraṇapaññatti asādhāraṇapaññatti, ekatopaññatti ubhatopaññatti, pañcannaṃ pātimokkhuddesānaṃ katthogadhaṃ kattha pariyāpannaṃ, katamena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchati, catunnaṃ vipattīnaṃ katamā vipatti, sattannaṃ āpattikkhandhānaṃ katamo āpattikkhandho, channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti, catunnaṃ adhikaraṇānaṃ katamaṃ adhikaraṇaṃ, sattannaṃ samathānaṃ katihi samathehi sammati, ko tattha vinayo, ko tattha abhivinayo, kiṃ tattha pātimokkhaṃ, kiṃ tattha adhipātimokkhaṃ, kā vipatti, kā sampatti, kā paṭipatti, kati atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā paṭhamo aniyato paññatto, ke {pb:T:0.0015} sikkhanti, ke sikkhitasikkhā, kattha ṭhitaṃ, ke dhārenti, kassa vacanaṃ kenābhatanti.

{para:22} 22\. Yaṃ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena paṭhamo aniyato kattha {pb:V:0.0012} paññattoti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā udāyī mātugāmena saddhiṃ eko ekāya raho paṭicchanne āsane alaṅkammaniye nisajjaṃ kappesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññattīti? Ekā paññatti. Anupaññatti anuppannapaññatti tasmiṃ natthi. Sabbatthapaññatti, padesapaññattīti? Sabbatthapaññatti. Sādhāraṇapaññatti, asādhāraṇapaññattīti? Asādhāraṇapaññatti. Ekatopaññatti, ubhatopaññattīti? Ekatopaññatti. Pañcannaṃ pātimokkhuddesānaṃ katthogadhaṃ kattha pariyāpannanti? Nidānogadhaṃ nidānapariyāpannaṃ. Katamena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchatīti? Catutthena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchati. Catunnaṃ vipattīnaṃ katamā vipattīti? Siyā sīlavipatti siyā ācāravipatti. Sattannaṃ āpattikkhandhānaṃ katamo āpattikkhandhoti? Siyā pārājikāpattikkhandho siyā saṅghādisesāpattikkhandho siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandho. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhātīti? Eke {pb:M:0.0012} samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca {pb:T:0.0016} cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato. Catunnaṃ adhikaraṇānaṃ katamaṃ adhikaraṇanti? Āpattādhikaraṇaṃ. Sattannaṃ samathānaṃ katihi samathehi sammatīti? Tīhi samathehi sammati – siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. Ko tattha vinayo, ko tattha abhivinayoti? Paññatti vinayo, vibhatti abhivinayo. Kiṃ tattha pātimokkhaṃ, kiṃ tattha adhipātimokkhanti? Paññatti pātimokkhaṃ, vibhatti adhipātimokkhaṃ. Kā vipattīti? Asaṃvaro vipatti. Kā sampattīti? Saṃvaro sampatti. Kā paṭipattīti? Na evarūpaṃ karissāmīti yāvajīvaṃ āpāṇakoṭikaṃ samādāya sikkhati sikkhāpadesu. {note:a. ni. 10.31} Kati atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā paṭhamo aniyato paññattoti{pb:P:5.0008}? Dasa atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā paṭhamo aniyato paññatto – saṅghasuṭṭhutāya, saṅghaphāsutāya, dummaṅkūnaṃ puggalānaṃ niggahāya, pesalānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ phāsuvihārāya, diṭṭhadhammikānaṃ āsavānaṃ saṃvarāya, samparāyikānaṃ āsavānaṃ paṭighātāya, appasannānaṃ pasādāya, pasannānaṃ bhiyyobhāvāya, saddhammaṭṭhitiyā, vinayānuggahāya. Ke sikkhantīti? Sekkhā ca puthujjanakalyāṇakā ca sikkhanti. Ke sikkhitasikkhāti? Arahanto sikkhitasikkhā. Kattha ṭhitanti? Sikkhākāmesu ṭhitaṃ. Ke dhārentīti? Yesaṃ vattati te dhārenti. Kassa vacananti? Bhagavato vacanaṃ arahato sammāsambuddhassa. Kenābhatanti? Paramparābhataṃ –

::gatha1
Upāli {pb:T:0.0017} dāsako ceva, soṇako siggavo tathā;
::

::gathalast
Moggaliputtena pañcamā, ete jambusirivhaye.
::

::gatha1
Tato {pb:V:0.0013} mahindo iṭṭiyo, uttiyo sambalo tathā;
::

::gathalast
Bhaddanāmo ca paṇḍito.
::

::gatha1
Ete nāgā mahāpaññā, jambudīpā idhāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Vinayaṃ te vācayiṃsu, piṭakaṃ tambapaṇṇiyā.
::

::gatha1
Nikāye pañca vācesuṃ, satta ceva pakaraṇe;
::

::gathalast
Tato ariṭṭho medhāvī, tissadatto ca paṇḍito.
::

::gatha1
Visārado kāḷasumano, thero ca dīghanāmako;
::

::gathalast
Dīghasumano ca paṇḍito.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva {pb:M:0.0013} kāḷasumano, nāgatthero ca buddharakkhito;
::

::gathalast
Tissatthero ca medhāvī, devatthero ca paṇḍito.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva sumano medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado;
::

::gathalast
Bahussuto cūḷanāgo, gajova duppadhaṃsiyo.
::

::gatha1
Dhammapālitanāmo ca, rohaṇe sādhupūjito;
::

::gathalast
Tassa sisso mahāpañño, khemanāmo tipeṭako.
::

::gatha1
Dīpe tārakarājāva paññāya atirocatha;
::

::gathalast
Upatisso ca medhāvī, phussadevo mahākathī.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva sumano medhāvī, pupphanāmo bahussuto;
::

::gathalast
Mahākathī mahāsivo, piṭake sabbattha kovido.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva upāli medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado;
::

::gathalast
Mahānāgo mahāpañño, saddhammavaṃsakovido.
::

::gatha1
Punadeva {pb:V:0.0014} abhayo medhāvī, piṭake sabbattha kovido;
::

::gathalast
Tissatthero ca medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado.
::

::gatha1
Tassa sisso mahāpañño, pupphanāmo bahussuto;
::

::gathalast
Sāsanaṃ anurakkhanto, jambudīpe patiṭṭhito.
::

::gatha1
Cūḷābhayo ca medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado;
::

::gathalast
Tissatthero ca medhāvī, saddhammavaṃsakovido.
::

::gatha1
Cūḷadevo ca medhāvī, vinaye ca visārado;
::

::gathalast
Sivatthero ca medhāvī, vinaye sabbattha kovido.
::

::gatha1
Ete nāgā mahāpaññā, vinayaññū maggakovidā;
::

::gathalast
Vinayaṃ dīpe pakāsesuṃ, piṭakaṃ tambapaṇṇiyāti.
::

{para:23} 23\. Yaṃ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena dutiyo aniyato kattha paññattoti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññatto. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā udāyī mātugāmena saddhiṃ eko ekāya raho nisajjaṃ kappesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti anuppannapaññattīti? Ekā paññatti. Anupaññatti {pb:M:0.0014} anuppannapaññatti tasmiṃ natthi. Sabbatthapaññatti, padesapaññattīti? Sabbatthapaññatti. Sādhāraṇapaññatti asādhāraṇapaññattīti? Asādhāraṇapaññatti. Ekatopaññatti ubhatopaññattīti? Ekatopaññatti. Pañcannaṃ pātimokkhuddesānaṃ katthogadhaṃ kattha pariyāpannanti? Nidānogadhaṃ nidānapariyāpannaṃ. Katamena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchatīti? Catutthena uddesena uddesaṃ āgacchati. Catunnaṃ vipattīnaṃ katamā vipattīti? Siyā sīlavipatti, siyā ācāravipatti. Sattannaṃ āpattikkhandhānaṃ katamo āpattikkhandhoti? Siyā {pb:T:0.0018} saṅghādisesāpattikkhandho, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandho. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhātīti? Tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti. Catunnaṃ adhikaraṇānaṃ katamaṃ adhikaraṇanti? Āpattādhikaraṇaṃ. Sattannaṃ samathānaṃ katihi samathehi sammatīti? Tīhi samathehi sammati – siyā {pb:V:0.0015} sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca…pe….

::centre
Dve aniyatā niṭṭhitā.
::

::centre
Tassuddānaṃ –
::

::gatha1
Alaṅkammaniyañceva, tatheva ca na heva kho;
::

::gathalast
Aniyatā supaññattā, buddhaseṭṭhena tādināti.
::

#### 4. Nissaggiyakaṇḍaṃ

#### 1. Kathinavaggo

{para:24} 24\. Yaṃ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena atirekacīvaraṃ dasāhaṃ atikkāmentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Vesāliyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū atirekacīvaraṃ dhāresuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi {pb:M:0.0015} samuṭṭhāti {pb:T:0.0019} – siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:25} 25\. Ekarattaṃ ticīvarena vippavasantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū bhikkhūnaṃ hatthe cīvaraṃ nikkhipitvā santaruttarena janapadacārikaṃ pakkamiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:26} 26\. Akālacīvaraṃ paṭiggahetvā māsaṃ atikkāmentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū akālacīvaraṃ paṭiggahetvā māsaṃ atikkāmesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti{pb:V:0.0016}, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:27} 27\. Aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā purāṇacīvaraṃ dhovāpentassa {pb:P:5.0009} nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā {pb:T:0.0020} udāyī aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā purāṇacīvaraṃ dhovāpesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:28} 28\. Aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā hatthato cīvaraṃ paṭiggaṇhantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā udāyī aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā hatthato cīvaraṃ paṭiggahesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:29} 29\. Aññātakaṃ {pb:M:0.0016} gahapatiṃ vā gahapatāniṃ vā cīvaraṃ viññāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto aññātakaṃ seṭṭhiputtaṃ cīvaraṃ viññāpesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:30} 30\. Aññātakaṃ gahapatiṃ vā gahapatāniṃ vā tatuttari cīvaraṃ viññāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū na mattaṃ jānitvā bahuṃ cīvaraṃ {pb:T:0.0021} viññāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:31} 31\. Pubbe appavāritassa aññātakaṃ gahapatikaṃ upasaṅkamitvā cīvare vikappaṃ āpajjantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando {pb:V:0.0017} sakyaputto pubbe appavārito aññātakaṃ gahapatikaṃ upasaṅkamitvā cīvare vikappaṃ āpajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:32} 32\. Pubbe appavāritassa aññātake gahapatike upasaṅkamitvā cīvare vikappaṃ āpajjantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto pubbe appavārito aññātake gahapatike upasaṅkamitvā cīvare vikappaṃ āpajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:33} 33\. Atirekatikkhattuṃ codanāya atirekachakkhattuṃ ṭhānena cīvaraṃ abhinipphādentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ {pb:T:0.0022}{pb:P:5.0010} paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto upāsakena – ‘‘ajjaṇho, bhante, āgamehī’’ti {pb:M:0.0017} vuccamāno nāgamesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Kathinavaggo paṭhamo.
::

#### 2. Kosiyavaggo

{para:34} 34\. Kosiyamissakaṃ santhataṃ kārāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Āḷaviyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū kosiyakārake upasaṅkamitvā evamāhaṃsu ‘‘bahū, āvuso, kosakārake pacatha. Amhākampi dassatha. Mayampi icchāma kosiyamissakaṃ santhataṃ kātu’’nti, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:35} 35\. Suddhakāḷakānaṃ eḷakalomānaṃ santhataṃ kārāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Vesāliyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti{pb:T:0.0023}? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū suddhakāḷakānaṃ eḷakalomānaṃ santhataṃ kārāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:36} 36\. Anādiyitvā {pb:V:0.0018} tulaṃ odātānaṃ tulaṃ gocariyānaṃ navaṃ santhataṃ kārāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū thokaññeva odātaṃ ante {note:odātānaṃ ante ante (sī.), odātānaṃ ante (syā.)} ādiyitvā tatheva suddhakāḷakānaṃ eḷakalomānaṃ santhataṃ kārāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:37} 37\. Anuvassaṃ santhataṃ kārāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū anuvassaṃ santhataṃ kārāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ{pb:M:0.0018}. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:38} 38\. Anādiyitvā purāṇasanthatassa sāmantā sugatavidatthiṃ navaṃ nisīdanasanthataṃ kārāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha{pb:T:0.0024}. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū santhatāni ujjhitvā āraññikaṅgaṃ piṇḍapātikaṅgaṃ paṃsukūlikaṅgaṃ samādiyiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:39} 39\. Eḷakalomāni paṭiggahetvā tiyojanaṃ atikkāmentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu eḷakalomāni paṭiggahetvā tiyojanaṃ atikkāmesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi {pb:P:5.0011} samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:40} 40\. Aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā eḷakalomāni dhovāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sakkesu paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū aññātikāhi bhikkhunīhi eḷakalomāni dhovāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:41} 41\. Rūpiyaṃ paṭiggaṇhantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ{pb:V:0.0019}. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ {pb:T:0.0025} sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto rūpiyaṃ paṭiggahesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:42} 42\. Nānappakārakaṃ rūpiyasaṃvohāraṃ samāpajjantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū {pb:M:0.0019} ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū nānappakārakaṃ rūpiyasaṃvohāraṃ samāpajjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:43} 43\. Nānappakārakaṃ kayavikkayaṃ samāpajjantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto paribbājakena saddhiṃ kayavikkayaṃ samāpajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Kosiyavaggo dutiyo.
::

#### 3. Pattavaggo

{para:44} 44\. Atirekapattaṃ {pb:T:0.0026} dasāhaṃ atikkāmentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū atirekapattaṃ dhāresuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:45} 45\. Ūnapañcabandhanena pattena aññaṃ navaṃ pattaṃ cetāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sakkesu paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū appamattakenapi bhinnena appamattakenapi khaṇḍena vilikhitamattenapi bahū patte viññāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:46} 46\. Bhesajjāni {pb:V:0.0020} paṭiggahetvā sattāhaṃ atikkāmentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū {pb:P:5.0012} ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū bhesajjāni paṭiggahetvā sattāhaṃ atikkāmesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:47} 47\. Atirekamāse {pb:T:0.0027}{pb:M:0.0020} sese gimhāne vassikasāṭikacīvaraṃ pariyesantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū atirekamāse sese gimhāne vassikasāṭikacīvaraṃ pariyesiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:48} 48\. Bhikkhussa sāmaṃ cīvaraṃ datvā kupitena anattamanena acchindantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto bhikkhussa sāmaṃ cīvaraṃ datvā kupito anattamano acchindi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:49} 49\. Sāmaṃ suttaṃ viññāpetvā tantavāyehi cīvaraṃ vāyāpentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū sāmaṃ suttaṃ viññāpetvā tantavāyehi cīvaraṃ vāyāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:50} 50\. Pubbe appavāritassa aññātakassa gahapatikassa tantavāye upasaṅkamitvā {pb:T:0.0028} cīvare vikappaṃ āpajjantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto pubbe appavārito aññātakassa gahapatikassa tantavāye upasaṅkamitvā cīvare vikappaṃ āpajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:51} 51\. Accekacīvaraṃ {pb:V:0.0021} paṭiggahetvā cīvarakālasamayaṃ atikkāmentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū accekacīvaraṃ paṭiggahetvā cīvarakālasamayaṃ atikkāmesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:52} 52\. Tiṇṇaṃ {pb:M:0.0021} cīvarānaṃ aññataraṃ cīvaraṃ antaraghare nikkhipitvā atirekachārattaṃ vippavasantassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū tiṇṇaṃ cīvarānaṃ aññataraṃ cīvaraṃ antaraghare nikkhipitvā atirekachārattaṃ vippavasiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā {pb:P:5.0013} paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:53} 53\. Jānaṃ {pb:T:0.0029} saṅghikaṃ lābhaṃ pariṇataṃ attano pariṇāmentassa nissaggiyaṃ pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū jānaṃ saṅghikaṃ lābhaṃ pariṇataṃ attano pariṇāmesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Pattavaggo tatiyo.
::

::centre
Tiṃsa nissaggiyā pācittiyā niṭṭhitā.
::

::centre
Tassuddānaṃ –
::

::gatha1
Dasekarattimāso ca, dhovanañca paṭiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Aññātaṃ tañca {note:aññātakañca (ka.)} uddissa, ubhinnaṃ dūtakena ca.
::

::gatha1
Kosiyā suddhadvebhāgā, chabbassāni nisīdanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dve ca lomāni uggaṇhe, ubho nānappakārakā.
::

::gatha1
Dve ca pattāni bhesajjaṃ, vassikā dānapañcamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaṃ vāyāpanacceko, sāsaṅkaṃ saṅghikena cāti.
::

#### 5. Pācittiyakaṇḍaṃ

#### 1. Musāvādavaggo

{para:54} 54\. Yaṃ {pb:V:0.0022} tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena sampajānamusāvāde pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti{pb:M:0.0022}? Hatthakaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha{pb:T:0.0030}. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā hatthako sakyaputto titthiyehi saddhiṃ sallapanto avajānitvā paṭijāni, paṭijānitvā avajāni, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:55} 55\. Omasavāde pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū pesalehi bhikkhūhi saddhiṃ bhaṇḍantā {note:bhaṇḍentā (ka.)} pesale bhikkhū omasiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:56} 56\. Bhikkhupesuññe pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhūnaṃ bhaṇḍanajātānaṃ kalahajātānaṃ vivādāpannānaṃ pesuññaṃ upasaṃhariṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:57} 57\. Anupasampannaṃ padaso dhammaṃ vācentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū {pb:T:0.0031} ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū upāsake padaso dhammaṃ vācesuṃ{pb:P:5.0014}, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā vācato samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato na cittato; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato…pe….

{para:58} 58\. Anupasampannena uttaridirattatirattaṃ sahaseyyaṃ kappentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Āḷaviyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū anupasampannena sahaseyyaṃ kappesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti{pb:V:0.0023}, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ {pb:M:0.0023} āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:59} 59\. Mātugāmena sahaseyyaṃ kappentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ anuruddhaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā anuruddho mātugāmena sahaseyyaṃ kappesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:60} 60\. Mātugāmassa uttarichappañcavācāhi dhammaṃ desentassa pācittiyaṃ {pb:T:0.0032} kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā udāyī mātugāmassa dhammaṃ desesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, dve anupaññattiyo. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti padasodhamme…pe….

{para:61} 61\. Anupasampannassa uttarimanussadhammaṃ bhūtaṃ ārocentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Vesāliyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Vaggumudātīriye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Vaggumudātīriyā bhikkhū gihīnaṃ aññamaññassa uttarimanussadhammassa vaṇṇaṃ bhāsiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; siyā vācato samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato na cittato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato…pe….

{para:62} 62\. Bhikkhussa duṭṭhullāpattiṃ anupasampannassa ārocentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhussa duṭṭhullāpattiṃ anupasampannassa ārocesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:63} 63\. Pathaviṃ {pb:T:0.0033} khaṇantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Āḷaviyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āḷavake bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āḷavakā {pb:M:0.0024} bhikkhū pathaviṃ khaṇiṃsu{pb:V:0.0024}, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Musāvādavaggo paṭhamo.
::

#### 2. Bhūtagāmavaggo

{para:64} 64\. Bhūtagāmapātabyatā {pb:P:5.0015} pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Āḷaviyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āḷavake bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āḷavakā bhikkhū rukkhaṃ chindiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:65} 65\. Aññavādake vihesake pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Kosambiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ channaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā channo saṅghamajjhe āpattiyā anuyuñjiyamāno aññenaññaṃ paṭicari, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ {pb:T:0.0034} tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:66} 66\. Ujjhāpanake khiyyanake pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Mettiyabhūmajake bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Mettiyabhūmajakā bhikkhū āyasmantaṃ dabbaṃ mallaputtaṃ bhikkhū ujjhāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:67} 67\. Saṅghikaṃ mañcaṃ vā pīṭhaṃ vā bhisiṃ vā kocchaṃ vā ajjhokāse santharitvā anuddharitvā anāpucchā pakkamantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū saṅghikaṃ senāsanaṃ ajjhokāse santharitvā anuddharitvā anāpucchā pakkamiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:68} 68\. Saṅghike {pb:M:0.0025} vihāre seyyaṃ santharitvā anuddharitvā anāpucchā pakkamantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sattarasavaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sattarasavaggiyā bhikkhū saṅghike vihāre seyyaṃ santharitvā anuddharitvā {pb:V:0.0025} anāpucchā pakkamiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti{pb:T:0.0035}. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:69} 69\. Saṅghike vihāre jānaṃ pubbupagataṃ bhikkhuṃ anupakhajja seyyaṃ kappentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū there bhikkhū anupakhajja seyyaṃ kappesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:70} 70\. Bhikkhuṃ kupitena anattamanena saṅghikā vihārā nikkaḍḍhantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū kupitā anattamanā bhikkhū saṅghikā vihārā nikkaḍḍhiṃsu{pb:P:5.0016}, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:71} 71\. Saṅghike vihāre uparivehāsakuṭiyā āhaccapādakaṃ mañcaṃ vā pīṭhaṃ vā abhinisīdantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu saṅghike vihāre uparivehāsakuṭiyā āhaccapādakaṃ mañcaṃ sahasā abhinisīdi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā {pb:T:0.0036} paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:72} 72\. Dvattipariyāye adhiṭṭhahitvā tatuttari adhiṭṭhahantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Kosambiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ channaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā channo katapariyositaṃ vihāraṃ punappunaṃ chādāpesi, punappunaṃ limpāpesi, atibhāriko vihāro paripati{pb:M:0.0026}, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:73} 73\. Jānaṃ sappāṇakaṃ udakaṃ tiṇaṃ vā mattikaṃ vā siñcantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Āḷaviyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āḷavake bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti{pb:V:0.0026}? Āḷavakā bhikkhū jānaṃ sappāṇakaṃ udakaṃ tiṇampi mattikampi siñciṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Bhūtagāmavaggo dutiyo.
::

#### 3. Ovādavaggo

{para:74} 74\. Asammatena {pb:T:0.0037} bhikkhuniyo ovadantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū asammatā bhikkhuniyo ovadiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññattīti? Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Anuppannapaññatti tasmiṃ natthi. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā vācato samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato na cittato; siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato…pe….

{para:75} 75\. Atthaṅgate sūriye bhikkhuniyo ovadantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ cūḷapanthakaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā cūḷapanthako atthaṅgate sūriye bhikkhuniyo ovadi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti padasodhamme…pe….

{para:76} 76\. Bhikkhunupassayaṃ upasaṅkamitvā bhikkhuniyo ovadantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sakkesu paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū {pb:T:0.0038} ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhunupassayaṃ {pb:P:5.0017} upasaṅkamitvā bhikkhuniyo ovadiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:77} 77\. ‘‘Āmisahetu {pb:M:0.0027} bhikkhū bhikkhuniyo ovadantī’’ti bhaṇantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū ‘‘āmisahetu bhikkhū bhikkhuniyo ovadantī’’ti bhaṇiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:78} 78\. Aññātikāya {pb:V:0.0027} bhikkhuniyā cīvaraṃ dentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā cīvaraṃ adāsi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:79} 79\. Aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā cīvaraṃ sibbentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā udāyī aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā cīvaraṃ sibbesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti {pb:T:0.0039} …pe….

{para:80} 80\. Bhikkhuniyā saddhiṃ saṃvidhāya ekaddhānamaggaṃ paṭipajjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhunīhi saddhiṃ saṃvidhāya ekaddhānamaggaṃ paṭipajjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ catūhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato; siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:81} 81\. Bhikkhuniyā saddhiṃ saṃvidhāya ekaṃ nāvaṃ abhiruhantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhunīhi saddhiṃ saṃvidhāya ekaṃ nāvaṃ abhiruhiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ catūhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:82} 82\. Jānaṃ {pb:M:0.0028} bhikkhuniparipācitaṃ piṇḍapātaṃ bhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Devadattaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Devadatto jānaṃ bhikkhuniparipācitaṃ {pb:T:0.0040} piṇḍapātaṃ bhuñji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:83} 83\. Bhikkhuniyā {pb:P:5.0018}{pb:V:0.0028} saddhiṃ eko ekāya raho nisajjaṃ kappentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā udāyī bhikkhuniyā saddhiṃ eko ekāya raho nisajjaṃ kappesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

::centre
Ovādavaggo tatiyo.
::

#### 4. Bhojanavaggo

{para:84} 84\. Tatuttari āvasathapiṇḍaṃ bhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū {pb:T:0.0041} ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū anuvasitvā anuvasitvā āvasathapiṇḍaṃ bhuñjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:85} 85\. Gaṇabhojane pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Devadattaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Devadatto sapariso kulesu viññāpetvā viññāpetvā bhuñji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, satta anupaññattiyo. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:86} 86\. Paramparabhojane pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Vesāliyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū {pb:M:0.0029} aññatra nimantitā aññatra bhuñjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, catasso anupaññattiyo. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:87} 87\. Dvattipattapūre pūve paṭiggahetvā tatuttari paṭiggaṇhantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū na mattaṃ jānitvā paṭiggahesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā {pb:T:0.0042} paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:88} 88\. Bhuttāvinā {pb:V:0.0029} pavāritena anatirittaṃ khādanīyaṃ vā bhojanīyaṃ vā bhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū bhuttāvī pavāritā aññatra bhuñjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:89} 89\. Bhikkhuṃ bhuttāviṃ pavāritaṃ anatirittena khādanīyena vā bhojanīyena vā abhihaṭṭhuṃ pavārentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu bhikkhuṃ bhuttāviṃ pavāritaṃ anatirittena bhojanīyena abhihaṭṭhuṃ pavāresi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:90} 90\. Vikāle {pb:P:5.0019} khādanīyaṃ vā bhojanīyaṃ vā bhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sattarasavaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sattarasavaggiyā bhikkhū vikāle bhojanaṃ bhuñjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:91} 91\. Sannidhikārakaṃ khādanīyaṃ vā bhojanīyaṃ vā bhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ belaṭṭhasīsaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā belaṭṭhasīso sannidhikārakaṃ bhojanaṃ {pb:M:0.0030} bhuñji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:92} 92\. Paṇītabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū paṇītabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ catūhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:93} 93\. Adinnaṃ mukhadvāraṃ āhāraṃ āharantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Vesāliyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu {pb:V:0.0030} adinnaṃ mukhadvāraṃ {pb:T:0.0044} āhāraṃ āhari, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

::centre
Bhojanavaggo catuttho.
::

#### 5. Acelakavaggo

{para:94} 94\. Acelakassa vā paribbājakassa vā paribbājikāya vā sahatthā khādanīyaṃ vā bhojanīyaṃ vā dentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Vesāliyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ ānandaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā ānando aññatarissā paribbājikāya ekaṃ maññamāno dve pūve adāsi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:95} 95\. Bhikkhuṃ ‘‘ehāvuso, gāmaṃ vā nigamaṃ vā piṇḍāya pavisissāmā’’ti tassa dāpetvā vā adāpetvā vā uyyojentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti{pb:T:0.0045}? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto bhikkhuṃ ‘‘ehāvuso, gāmaṃ piṇḍāya pavisissāmā’’ti, tassa adāpetvā uyyojesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:96} 96\. Sabhojane {pb:M:0.0031} kule anupakhajja nisajjaṃ kappentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto sabhojane kule anupakhajja nisajjaṃ kappesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti{pb:P:5.0020}. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:97} 97\. Mātugāmena saddhiṃ raho paṭicchanne āsane nisajjaṃ kappentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto mātugāmena saddhiṃ raho paṭicchanne āsane nisajjaṃ kappesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:98} 98\. Mātugāmena {pb:V:0.0031} saddhiṃ eko ekāya raho nisajjaṃ kappentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto mātugāmena saddhiṃ eko ekāya raho nisajjaṃ kappesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:99} 99\. Nimantitena sabhattena santaṃ bhikkhuṃ anāpucchā purebhattaṃ pacchābhattaṃ kulesu cārittaṃ āpajjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto nimantito sabhatto samāno purebhattaṃ pacchābhattaṃ kulesu cārittaṃ āpajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, catasso anupaññattiyo. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:100} 100\. Tatuttari bhesajjaṃ viññāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sakkesu paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū mahānāmena sakkena ‘‘ajjaṇho, bhante, āgamethā’’ti {pb:M:0.0032} vuccamānā nāgamesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:101} 101\. Uyyuttaṃ senaṃ dassanāya gacchantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti{pb:T:0.0047}? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū uyyuttaṃ senaṃ dassanāya agamaṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:102} 102\. Atirekatirattaṃ senāya vasantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū atirekatirattaṃ senāya vasiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:103} 103\. Uyyodhikaṃ gacchantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ{pb:P:5.0021}. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū uyyodhikaṃ {pb:V:0.0032} agamaṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

::centre
Acelakavaggo pañcamo.
::

#### 6. Surāpānavaggo

{para:104} 104\. Surāmerayapāne {pb:T:0.0048} pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Kosambiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ sāgataṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā sāgato majjaṃ pivi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:105} 105\. Aṅgulipatodake pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā {pb:M:0.0033} bhikkhū bhikkhuṃ aṅgulipatodakena hāsesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:106} 106\. Udake hasadhamme {note:hassadhamme (sī. syā.)} pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sattarasavaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sattarasavaggiyā bhikkhū aciravatiyā nadiyā udake kīḷiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato {pb:T:0.0049} ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:107} 107\. Anādariye pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Kosambiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ channaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā channo anādariyaṃ akāsi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:108} 108\. Bhikkhuṃ bhiṃsāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhuṃ bhiṃsāpesuṃ{pb:V:0.0033}, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:109} 109\. Jotiṃ samādahitvā visibbentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Bhaggesu paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū jotiṃ samādahitvā visibbesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, dve anupaññattiyo. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:110} 110\. Orenaddhamāsaṃ nahāyantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū rājānampi passitvā na {pb:T:0.0050} mattaṃ jānitvā nahāyiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, cha anupaññattiyo. Sabbatthapaññatti, padesapaññattīti? Padesapaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:111} 111\. Anādiyitvā {pb:P:5.0022}{pb:M:0.0034} tiṇṇaṃ dubbaṇṇakaraṇānaṃ aññataraṃ dubbaṇṇakaraṇaṃ navaṃ cīvaraṃ paribhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū attano cīvaraṃ na sañjāniṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti eḷakalomake…pe….

{para:112} 112\. Bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā sikkhamānāya vā sāmaṇerassa vā sāmaṇeriyā vā sāmaṃ cīvaraṃ vikappetvā appaccuddhāraṇaṃ paribhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto bhikkhussa sāmaṃ cīvaraṃ vikappetvā appaccuddhāraṇaṃ paribhuñji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:113} 113\. Bhikkhussa pattaṃ vā cīvaraṃ vā nisīdanaṃ vā sūcigharaṃ vā kāyabandhanaṃ vā apanidhentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ {pb:T:0.0051} paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhūnaṃ pattampi cīvarampi apanidhesuṃ{pb:V:0.0034}, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Surāmerayavaggo chaṭṭho.
::

#### 7. Sappāṇakavaggo

{para:114} 114\. Sañcicca pāṇaṃ jīvitā voropentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ udāyiṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā udāyī sañcicca pāṇaṃ jīvitā voropesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:115} 115\. Jānaṃ sappāṇakaṃ udakaṃ paribhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti{pb:M:0.0035}? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū jānaṃ sappāṇakaṃ {pb:T:0.0052} udakaṃ paribhuñjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:116} 116\. Jānaṃ yathādhammaṃ nihatādhikaraṇaṃ puna kammāya ukkoṭentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū jānaṃ yathādhammaṃ nihatādhikaraṇaṃ puna kammāya ukkoṭesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:117} 117\. Bhikkhussa jānaṃ duṭṭhullaṃ āpattiṃ paṭicchādentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ {pb:P:5.0023} ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu bhikkhussa jānaṃ duṭṭhullaṃ āpattiṃ paṭicchādesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:118} 118\. Jānaṃ ūnavīsativassaṃ puggalaṃ upasampādentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule {pb:V:0.0035} bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū jānaṃ ūnavīsativassaṃ puggalaṃ upasampādesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:119} 119\. Jānaṃ {pb:T:0.0053} theyyasatthena saddhiṃ saṃvidhāya ekaddhānamaggaṃ paṭipajjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu jānaṃ theyyasatthena saddhiṃ saṃvidhāya ekaddhānamaggaṃ paṭipajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:120} 120\. Mātugāmena saddhiṃ saṃvidhāya ekaddhānamaggaṃ paṭipajjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ {pb:M:0.0036} vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu mātugāmena saddhiṃ saṃvidhāya ekaddhānamaggaṃ paṭipajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ catūhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:121} 121\. Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā yāvatatiyaṃ samanubhāsanāya na paṭinissajjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Ariṭṭhaṃ bhikkhuṃ gaddhabādhipubbaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Ariṭṭho bhikkhu gaddhabādhipubbo pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā yāvatatiyaṃ samanubhāsanāya na paṭinissajji, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti. Kāyato ca vācato {pb:T:0.0054} ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:122} 122\. Jānaṃ tathāvādinā bhikkhunā {note:ariṭṭhena bhikkhunā (ka.)} akaṭānudhammena taṃ diṭṭhiṃ appaṭinissaṭṭhena saddhiṃ sambhuñjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū jānaṃ tathāvādinā ariṭṭhena bhikkhunā akaṭānudhammena taṃ diṭṭhiṃ appaṭinissaṭṭhena saddhiṃ sambhuñjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:123} 123\. Jānaṃ tathānāsitaṃ samaṇuddesaṃ upalāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā {pb:V:0.0036} bhikkhū jānaṃ tathānāsitaṃ kaṇṭakaṃ {pb:P:5.0024} samaṇuddesaṃ upalāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Sappāṇakavaggo sattamo.
::

#### 8. Sahadhammikavaggo

{para:124} 124\. Bhikkhūhi {pb:T:0.0055} sahadhammikaṃ vuccamānena ‘‘na tāvāhaṃ, āvuso, etasmiṃ sikkhāpade sikkhissāmi yāva na aññaṃ bhikkhuṃ byattaṃ vinayadharaṃ paripucchissāmī’’ti {pb:M:0.0037} bhaṇantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Kosambiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ channaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā channo bhikkhūhi sahadhammikaṃ vuccamāno ‘‘na tāvāhaṃ, āvuso, etasmiṃ sikkhāpade sikkhissāmi yāva na aññaṃ bhikkhuṃ byattaṃ vinayadharaṃ paripucchissāmī’’ti bhaṇi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:125} 125\. Vinayaṃ vivaṇṇentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū vinayaṃ vivaṇṇesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:126} 126\. Mohanake pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū mohesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:127} 127\. Bhikkhussa kupitena anattamanena pahāraṃ dentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha {pb:T:0.0056} paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū kupitā anattamanā bhikkhūnaṃ pahāraṃ adaṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:128} 128\. Bhikkhussa kupitena anattamanena talasattikaṃ uggirantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti{pb:V:0.0037}? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū kupitā anattamanā bhikkhūnaṃ talasattikaṃ uggiriṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:129} 129\. Bhikkhuṃ amūlakena saṅghādisesena anuddhaṃsentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha{pb:M:0.0038}. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhuṃ amūlakena saṅghādisesena anuddhaṃsesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:130} 130\. Bhikkhussa sañcicca kukkuccaṃ upadahantassa {note:uppādentassa (syā.)} pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye {pb:T:0.0057} bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhūnaṃ sañcicca kukkuccaṃ upadahiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:131} 131\. Bhikkhūnaṃ bhaṇḍanajātānaṃ kalahajātānaṃ vivādāpannānaṃ {pb:P:5.0025} upassutiṃ {note:upassuti (?)} tiṭṭhantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhūnaṃ bhaṇḍanajātānaṃ kalahajātānaṃ vivādāpannānaṃ upassutiṃ tiṭṭhahiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:132} 132\. Dhammikānaṃ kammānaṃ chandaṃ datvā pacchā khīyanadhammaṃ {note:khiyyadhammaṃ (ka.)} āpajjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū dhammikānaṃ kammānaṃ chandaṃ datvā pacchā khīyanadhammaṃ āpajjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:133} 133\. Saṅghe vinicchayakathāya vattamānāya chandaṃ adatvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkamantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ{pb:T:0.0058}. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha{pb:V:0.0038}. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu saṅghe vinicchayakathāya vattamānāya chandaṃ adatvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkāmi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:134} 134\. Samagge {pb:M:0.0039} saṅghena cīvaraṃ datvā pacchā khīyanadhammaṃ āpajjantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū samaggena saṅghena cīvaraṃ datvā pacchā khīyanadhammaṃ āpajjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:135} 135\. Jānaṃ saṅghikaṃ lābhaṃ pariṇataṃ puggalassa pariṇāmentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū jānaṃ saṅghikaṃ lābhaṃ pariṇataṃ puggalassa pariṇāmesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Sahadhammikavaggo aṭṭhamo.
::

#### 9. Rājavaggo

{para:136} 136\. Pubbe {pb:T:0.0059} appaṭisaṃviditena rañño antepuraṃ pavisantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ ānandaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā ānando pubbe appaṭisaṃvidito rañño antepuraṃ pāvisi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:137} 137\. Ratanaṃ uggaṇhantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ{pb:P:5.0026}. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu ratanaṃ uggahesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, dve anupaññattiyo. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:138} 138\. Santaṃ bhikkhuṃ anāpucchā vikāle gāmaṃ pavisantassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti{pb:V:0.0039}? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū vikāle gāmaṃ pavisiṃsu, tasmiṃ {pb:T:0.0060} vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, tisso anupaññattiyo. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti kathinake…pe….

{para:139} 139\. Aṭṭhimayaṃ {pb:M:0.0040} vā dantamayaṃ vā visāṇamayaṃ vā sūcigharaṃ kārāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sakkesu paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū na mattaṃ jānitvā bahū sūcighare viññāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:140} 140\. Pamāṇātikkantaṃ mañcaṃ vā pīṭhaṃ vā kārāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ upanandaṃ sakyaputtaṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā upanando sakyaputto ucce mañce sayi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:141} 141\. Mañcaṃ vā pīṭhaṃ vā tūlonaddhaṃ kārāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū mañcaṃ vā pīṭhaṃ vā tūlonaddhaṃ kārāpesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:142} 142\. Pamāṇātikkantaṃ {pb:T:0.0061} nisīdanaṃ kārāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū appamāṇikāni nisīdanāni dhāresuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:143} 143\. Pamāṇātikkantaṃ kaṇḍuppaṭicchādiṃ kārāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū appamāṇikāyo kaṇḍuppaṭicchādiyo dhāresuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:144} 144\. Pamāṇātikkantaṃ {pb:V:0.0040} vassikasāṭikaṃ kārāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha{pb:M:0.0041}. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū appamāṇikāyo vassikasāṭikāyo dhāresuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:145} 145\. Sugatacīvarappamāṇaṃ {pb:P:5.0027} cīvaraṃ kārāpentassa pācittiyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Āyasmantaṃ nandaṃ {pb:T:0.0062} ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Āyasmā nando sugatacīvarappamāṇaṃ cīvaraṃ dhāresi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Rājavaggo navamo.
::

::centre
Dvenavuti pācittiyā niṭṭhitā.
::

::centre
Khuddakaṃ samattaṃ.
::

::centre
Tassuddānaṃ –
::

::gatha1
Musā omasapesuññaṃ, padaseyyā ca itthiyā;
::

::gathalast
Aññatra viññunā bhūtā {note:desanārocanā ceva (sī. syā.)}, duṭṭhullāpatti khaṇanā.
::

::gatha1
Bhūtaṃ aññāya ujjhāyi {note:bhūtaññavādaujjhāyi (sī.)}, mañco seyyo ca vuccati;
::

::gathalast
Pubbe nikkaḍḍhanāhacca, dvāraṃ sappāṇakena ca.
::

::gatha1
Asammatā atthaṅgate, upassayāmisena ca;
::

::gathalast
Dade sibbe vidhānena, nāvā bhuñjeyya ekato.
::

::gatha1
Piṇḍaṃ gaṇaṃ paraṃ pūvaṃ, pavārito pavāritaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vikālaṃ sannidhi khīraṃ, dantaponena te dasa.
::

::gatha1
Acelakaṃ uyyokhajja {note:acelakānupakhajja (ka.)}, paṭicchannaṃ rahena ca;
::

::gathalast
Nimantito paccayehi, senāvasanuyyodhikaṃ.
::

::gatha1
Surā {pb:V:0.0041} aṅguli hāso ca, anādariyañca bhiṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Joti nahāna dubbaṇṇaṃ, sāmaṃ apanidhena ca.
::

::gatha1
Sañciccudakakammā {pb:M:0.0042} ca, duṭṭhullaṃ ūnavīsati;
::

::gathalast
Theyyaitthiavadesaṃ {note:ariṭṭhakaṃ (vibhaṅge)}, saṃvāse nāsitena ca.
::

::gatha1
Sahadhammikavilekhā, moho pahārenuggire;
::

::gathalast
Amūlakañca sañcicca, sossāmi khiyyapakkame.
::

::gatha1
Saṅghena cīvaraṃ datvā, pariṇāmeyya puggale;
::

::gatha2
Raññañca ratanaṃ santaṃ, sūci mañco ca tūlikā;
::

::gathalast
Nisīdanaṃ kaṇḍucchādi, vassikā sugatena cāti.
::

::centre
Tesaṃ vaggānaṃ uddānaṃ –
::

::gatha1
Musā bhūtā ca ovādo, bhojanācelakena ca;
::

::gathalast
Surā sappāṇakā dhammo, rājavaggena te navāti.
::

#### 6. Pāṭidesanīyakaṇḍaṃ

{para:146} 146\. Yaṃ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā antaragharaṃ paviṭṭhāya hatthato khādanīyaṃ vā bhojanīyaṃ vā sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjantassa pāṭidesanīyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Aññataraṃ {pb:T:0.0063} bhikkhuṃ ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Aññataro bhikkhu aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā antaragharaṃ paviṭṭhāya hatthato āmisaṃ paṭiggahesi, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi {pb:P:5.0028} samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:147} 147\. Bhikkhuniyā vosāsantiyā na nivāretvā bhuñjantassa pāṭidesanīyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Rājagahe paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū bhikkhuniyo vosāsantiyo na nivāresuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā {pb:V:0.0042} paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

{para:148} 148\. Sekkhasammatesu {pb:M:0.0043} kulesu khādanīyaṃ vā bhojanīyaṃ vā sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjantassa pāṭidesanīyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū na mattaṃ jānitvā paṭiggahesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, dve anupaññattiyo. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; siyā kāyato ca cittato {pb:T:0.0064} ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

{para:149} 149\. Āraññakesu senāsanesu pubbe appaṭisaṃviditaṃ khādanīyaṃ vā bhojanīyaṃ vā ajjhārāme sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjantassa pāṭidesanīyaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sakkesu paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti. Sambahulā bhikkhū ārāme core paṭivasante nārocesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

::centre
Cattāro pāṭidesanīyā niṭṭhitā.
::

::centre
Tassuddānaṃ –
::

::gatha1
Aññātikāya vosāsaṃ, sekkhaāraññakena ca;
::

::gathalast
Pāṭidesanīyā cattāro, sambuddhena pakāsitāti.
::

#### 7. Sekhiyakaṇḍaṃ

#### 1. Parimaṇḍalavaggo

{para:150} 150\. Yaṃ {pb:V:0.0043} tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena anādariyaṃ paṭicca purato vā pacchato vā olambentena nivāsentassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū puratopi pacchatopi olambentā nivāsesuṃ, tasmiṃ {pb:T:0.0065} vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ {pb:M:0.0044} ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca purato vā pacchato vā olambentena pārupantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū puratopi pacchatopi olambentā pārupiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca kāyaṃ vivaritvā antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:P:5.0029} paṭicca kāyaṃ vivaritvā antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca hatthaṃ vā pādaṃ vā kīḷāpentena antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… {pb:T:0.0066} ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca hatthaṃ vā pādaṃ vā kīḷāpentena antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ {pb:V:0.0044} …pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca tahaṃ tahaṃ olokentena antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca tahaṃ tahaṃ olokentena antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca ukkhittakāya antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:M:0.0045} paṭicca ukkhittakāya antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena {pb:T:0.0067} samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

::centre
Parimaṇḍalavaggo paṭhamo.
::

#### 2. Ujjagghikavaggo

{para:151} 151\. Anādariyaṃ paṭicca ujjagghikāya antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū mahāhasitaṃ hasantā antaraghare gacchiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca ujjagghikāya antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā {pb:V:0.0045} bhikkhū mahāhasitaṃ hasantā antaraghare nisīdiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca uccāsaddaṃ mahāsaddaṃ karontena antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū uccāsaddaṃ mahāsaddaṃ karontā antaraghare gacchiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca uccāsaddaṃ mahāsaddaṃ karontena antaraghare {pb:T:0.0068} nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū uccāsaddaṃ mahāsaddaṃ karontā antaraghare nisīdiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti{pb:M:0.0046}. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca kāyappacālakaṃ antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca kāyappacālakaṃ antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca bāhuppacālakaṃ antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca bāhuppacālakaṃ antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti{pb:V:0.0046}. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sīsappacālakaṃ antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sīsappacālakaṃ antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti {pb:T:0.0069} – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Ujjagghikavaggo dutiyo.

#### 3. Khambhakatavaggo

{para:152} 152\. Anādariyaṃ paṭicca khambhakatena antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti. Kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:M:0.0047} paṭicca khambhakatena antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca oguṇṭhitena antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā {pb:V:0.0047} bhikkhū sasīsaṃ pārupitvā antaraghare gacchiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca oguṇṭhitena antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū sasīsaṃ pārupitvā antaraghare nisīdiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca ukkuṭikāya antaraghare gacchantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca pallatthikāya {note:pallattikāya (ka.)} antaraghare nisīdantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti {pb:T:0.0070} – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:P:5.0030} paṭicca asakkaccaṃ piṇḍapātaṃ paṭiggaṇhantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca tahaṃ tahaṃ olokentena piṇḍapātaṃ paṭiggaṇhantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sūpaññeva bahuṃ paṭiggaṇhantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:M:0.0048} paṭicca thūpīkataṃ piṇḍapātaṃ paṭiggaṇhantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

::centre
Khambhakatavaggo tatiyo.
::

#### 4. Piṇḍapātavaggo

{para:153} 153\. Anādariyaṃ {pb:V:0.0048} paṭicca asakkaccaṃ piṇḍapātaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca tahaṃ tahaṃ olokentena piṇḍapātaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:T:0.0071} paṭicca tahaṃ tahaṃ omasitvā piṇḍapātaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sūpaññeva bahuṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca thūpakato omadditvā piṇḍapātaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sūpaṃ vā byañjanaṃ vā odanena paṭicchādentassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sūpaṃ vā odanaṃ vā agilāno attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū sūpampi odanampi attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjiṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā {pb:M:0.0049} paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ dvīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti – siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:T:0.0072}{pb:V:0.0049} paṭicca ujjhānasaññinā paresaṃ pattaṃ olokentassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca mahantaṃ kabaḷaṃ karontassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca dīghaṃ ālopaṃ karontassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

::centre
Piṇḍapātavaggo catuttho.
::

#### 5. Kabaḷavaggo

{para:154} 154\. Anādariyaṃ paṭicca anāhaṭe kabaḷe mukhadvāraṃ vivarantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca bhuñjamānena sabbaṃ hatthaṃ mukhe pakkhipantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sakabaḷena mukhena byāharantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha{pb:P:5.0031}. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Chabbaggiyā bhikkhū sakabaḷena mukhena byāhariṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:M:0.0050} paṭicca piṇḍukkhepakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā {pb:T:0.0073} paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:V:0.0050} paṭicca kabaḷāvacchedakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca avagaṇḍakārakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca hatthaniddhunakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sitthāvakārakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca jivhānicchārakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca capucapukārakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

::centre
Kabaḷavaggo pañcamo.
::

#### 6. Surusuruvaggo

{para:155} 155\. Anādariyaṃ {pb:T:0.0074} paṭicca surusurukārakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Kosambiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū surusurukārakaṃ khīraṃ piviṃsu, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ{pb:M:0.0051}. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca hatthanillehakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ {pb:V:0.0051} paṭicca pattanillehakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca oṭṭhanillehakaṃ bhuñjantassa dukkaṭaṃ…pe… ekā paññatti. Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sāmisena hatthena pānīyathālakaṃ paṭiggaṇhantassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Bhaggesu paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū sāmisena hatthena pānīyathālakaṃ paṭiggahesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena {pb:T:0.0075} samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca sasitthakaṃ pattadhovanaṃ antaraghare chaḍḍentassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Bhaggesu paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti? Sambahulā bhikkhū sasitthakaṃ pattadhovanaṃ antaraghare chaḍḍesuṃ, tasmiṃ vatthusmiṃ. Ekā paññatti. Channaṃ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṃ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti – kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato…pe….

Anādariyaṃ paṭicca chattapāṇissa dhammaṃ desentassa dukkaṭaṃ kattha paññattanti? Sāvatthiyaṃ paññattaṃ. Kaṃ ārabbhāti? Chabbaggiye bhikkhū ārabbha. Kismiṃ vatthusminti?
